gsave
/bufferR %d string def
/bufferG %d string def
/bufferB %d string def
DjVuColorSpace setcolorspace
<< /ImageType 1
   /Width %d
   /Height %d
   /BitsPerComponent 8
   /Decode [0 1 0 1 0 1]
   /ImageMatrix [1 0 0 1 0 0]
   /MultipleDataSources true
   /DataSource [ { ReadR } { ReadG } { ReadB } ]
   /Interpolate false >> image
DjVuColorSpace setcolorspace
<< /ImageType 1
   /Width %d
   /Height %d
   /BitsPerComponent 8
   /Decode [0 1]
   /ImageMatrix [1 0 0 1 0 0]
   /DataSource currentfile /ASCII85Decode
       filter /RunLengthDecode filter
   /Interpolate false >> image
%% --- now doing a level 1 image
gsave
%d %d 8 [ 1 0 0 1 0 0 ]
{ ColorProc } false 3 ColorImage
%d %d 8 [ 1 0 0 1 0 0 ]
{ currentfile buffer8 readhexstring pop } image
%d %d 1 [ 1 0 0 1 0 0 ]
{ currentfile buffer8 readhexstring pop } image
%% --- now doing the background
gsave -%d -%d translate
/bgred %d def bgred bgred scale
DjVuColorSpace setcolorspace
<< /ImageType 1
   /Width %d
   /Height %d
   /BitsPerComponent 8
   /Decode [0 1]
   /ImageMatrix [1 0 0 1 0 0]
   /DataSource currentfile /ASCII85Decode
      filter /RunLengthDecode filter
   /Interpolate false >> image
/P {
  11 dict dup begin 4 1 roll
    /PatternType 1 def
    /PaintType 1 def
    /TilingType 1 def
    /H exch def
    /W exch def
    /Red %d def
    /PatternString exch def
    /XStep W Red mul def
    /YStep H Red mul def
    /BBox [0 0 XStep YStep] def
    /PaintProc { begin
       Red dup scale
       << /ImageType 1 /Width W /Height H
          /BitsPerComponent 8 /Interpolate false
          /Decode [%s] /ImageMatrix [1 0 0 1 0 0]
          /DataSource PatternString >> image
       end } bind def
     0 0 XStep YStep rectclip
     end matrix makepattern
  /Pattern setcolorspace setpattern
  0 0 moveto
} def
%% --- now doing the foreground
gsave DjVuColorSpace setcolorspace
/$DjVuLocalFont 7 dict def
$DjVuLocalFont begin
/FontType 3 def 
/FontMatrix [1 0 0 1 0 0] def
/FontBBox [0 0 1 .5] def
/CharStrings %d dict def
/Encoding 2 array def
0 1 1 {Encoding exch /.notdef put} for 
CharStrings begin
/.notdef {} def
/BuildGlyph {
  exch /CharStrings get exch
  2 copy known not
  {pop /.notdef} if
  get exec 
} bind def
/LocalDjVuFont $DjVuLocalFont definefont pop
/LocalDjVuFont findfont setfont
/LocalDjVuFont undefinefont grestore

image-width image-height rectstroke
grestore

      0 setgray 0.5 setlinewidth -36 0 moveto 0 0 lineto
      0 -36 lineto stroke grestore } bind def
0 0 0 cm 180 image-width image-height cm

%% -- coordinate system
/image-dpi %d def
/image-x 0 def
/image-y 0 def
/image-width  %d def
/image-height %d def

/a11 coeff def

/a23 0 def

%% -- begin printing
/page-origstate save def
%% -- coordinate system
/auto-orient %s def
/portrait %s def
/fit-page %s def
/zoom %d def
/image-dpi %d def
clippath pathbbox newpath
2 index sub exch 3 index sub
/page-width exch def
/page-height exch def
/page-y exch def
/page-x exch def
/image-x 0 def
/image-y 0 def
/image-width  %d def
/image-height %d def
/margin %d def
/halign %d def
/valign 0 def
%% -- position page
auto-orient {
  image-height image-width sub
  page-height page-width sub
  mul 0 ge /portrait exch def
} if
fit-page {
  /page-width page-width margin sub
     halign 0 eq { margin sub } if def
  /page-height page-height margin sub
     valign 0 eq { margin sub } if def
  /page-x page-x halign 0 ge { margin add } if def
  /page-y page-y valign 0 ge { margin add } if def
} if
portrait {
  fit-page {
    image-height page-height div
    image-width page-width div
    gt {
      page-height image-height div /coeff exch def
    } {
      page-width image-width div /coeff exch def
    } ifelse
  } {
    /coeff 72 image-dpi div zoom mul 100 div def
  } ifelse
  /start-x page-x page-width image-width
    coeff mul sub 2 div halign 1 add mul add def
  /start-y page-y page-height image-height
    coeff mul sub 2 div valign 1 add mul add def
  /a11 coeff def
  /a12 0 def
  /a13 start-x def
  /a21 0 def
  /a22 coeff def
  /a23 start-y def
} { %% landscape
  fit-page {
    image-height page-width div
    image-width page-height div
    gt {
      page-width image-height div /coeff exch def
    } {
      page-height image-width div /coeff exch def
    } ifelse
  } {
    /coeff 72 image-dpi div zoom mul 100 div def
  } ifelse
  /start-x page-x page-width add page-width image-height
    coeff mul sub 2 div valign 1 add mul sub def
  /start-y page-y page-height image-width
    coeff mul sub 2 div halign 1 add mul add def
  /a11 0 def
  /a12 coeff neg def
  /a13 start-x image-y coeff neg mul sub def
  /a21 coeff def
  /a22 0 def
  /a23 start-y image-x coeff mul add def 
} ifelse
[a11 a21 a12 a22 a13 a23] concat
gsave 0 0 image-width image-height rectclip
%% -- begin print
%%%%Page: (%d,%d) %d
gsave
/fold-dict 8 dict dup 3 1 roll def begin
 clippath pathbbox newpath pop pop translate
 clippath pathbbox newpath 4 2 roll pop pop
 /ph exch def
 /pw exch def
 /w ph %d sub 2 div def
 /m1 %d def
 /m2 %d def
%% -- folding marks
fold-dict begin
 0 setgray 0.5 setlinewidth
 ph m1 m2 add add 2 div dup
 0 exch moveto 36 0 rlineto stroke
 pw exch moveto -36 0 rlineto stroke
%% -- first page
gsave fold-dict begin
 0 ph 2 div w add m1 add translate 270 rotate
 0 0 w pw rectclip end
grestore

 0 ph 2 div m2 add translate 270 rotate
 0 0 w pw rectclip end

%% -- procs for reading color image
/readR () def
/readG () def
/readB () def
/ReadData {
   currentfile /ASCII85Decode filter dup
   /RunLengthDecode filter
   bufferR readstring pop /readR exch def
   dup status { flushfile } { pop } ifelse
   currentfile /ASCII85Decode filter dup
   /RunLengthDecode filter
   bufferG readstring pop /readG exch def
   dup status { flushfile } { pop } ifelse
   currentfile /ASCII85Decode filter dup
   /RunLengthDecode filter
   bufferB readstring pop /readB exch def
   dup status { flushfile } { pop } ifelse
} bind def
/ReadR {
   readR length 0 eq { ReadData } if
   readR /readR () def
} bind def
/ReadG {
   readG length 0 eq { ReadData } if
   readG /readG () def
} bind def
/ReadB {
   readB length 0 eq { ReadData } if
   readB /readB () def
} bind def
%% -- procs for foreground layer
/g {gsave 0 0 0 0 5 index 5 index setcachedevice
    true [1 0 0 1 0 0] 5 4 roll imagemask grestore
} bind def
/gn {gsave 0 0 0 0 6 index 6 index setcachedevice
  true [1 0 0 1 0 0] 3 2 roll 5 1 roll 
  { 1 sub 0 index 2 add 1 index  1 add roll
  } imagemask grestore pop 
} bind def
/c {setcolor rmoveto glyphshow} bind def
/s {rmoveto glyphshow} bind def
/S {rmoveto gsave show grestore} bind def
/F {(Helvetica) findfont exch scalefont setfont} bind def
%% -- emulations
systemdict /rectstroke known not {
  /rectstroke  %% stack : x y width height 
  { newpath 4 2 roll moveto 1 index 0 rlineto
    0 exch rlineto neg 0 rlineto closepath stroke
  } bind def } if
systemdict /rectclip known not {
  /rectclip  %% stack : x y width height 
  { newpath 4 2 roll moveto 1 index 0 rlineto
    0 exch rlineto neg 0 rlineto closepath clip
  } bind def } if
%% -- color space
/DjVuColorSpace [ %s
<< /DecodeLMN [ { dup 0.03928 le {
       12.92321 div
     } {
       0.055 add 1.055 div 2.4 exp
     } ifelse } bind dup dup ]
   /MatrixLMN [
      0.412457 0.212673 0.019334
      0.357576 0.715152 0.119192
      0.180437 0.072175 0.950301 ]
   /WhitePoint [ 0.9505 1 1.0890 ] %% D65 
   /BlackPoint[0 0 0] >> ] def
/DjVuColorSpace /DeviceRGB def
/DjVuColorSpace /DeviceGray def
%% -- buffers for reading image
/buffer8 () def
/buffer24 () def
%% -- colorimage emulation
systemdict /colorimage known {
   /ColorProc {
      currentfile buffer24 readhexstring pop
   } bind def
   /ColorImage {
      colorimage
   } bind def
   /ColorProc {
      currentfile buffer24 readhexstring pop
      /data exch def /datalen data length def
      /cnt 0 def
      0 1 datalen 3 idiv 1 sub {
         buffer8 exch
                data cnt get 20 mul /cnt cnt 1 add def
                data cnt get 32 mul /cnt cnt 1 add def
                data cnt get 12 mul /cnt cnt 1 add def
                add add 64 idiv put
      } for
      buffer8 0 datalen 3 idiv getinterval
   } bind def
   /ColorImage {
      pop pop image
   } bind def
} ifelse
